270b7(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs so ni/ kha sbyor ba'i rang bzhin nyid kyis mtha' dag nyid du khyab pa'o// // rab tu gsal ba'i kha sbyor gyi rgya cher 'grel pa las/ dgyes 
270b8(rgyud 'grel): pa'i rdo rje'i brgyud chen po rdzogs s+ho// @#/ le'u nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o// / zung du 'jug pa'i rim par grub pa zhal brgyad la sbyor ba/ 
271a1(rgyud 'grel): he ru ka'i bzang po gsal ba 'di ni bshad pa las// gang zhig dge ba bsags pa des ni dgyes rdor rnal 'byor gyis// sems ca
271a2(rgyud 'grel): rnams kyi srid pa rnam dag dngos grub sdong du shog// rab tu gsal ba'i kha sbyor gyi rgya cher 'grel pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon kA ya s+tha bgres po'i 
271a3(rgyud 'grel): zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs s+ho// rgya gar gyi mkhan po swA d+ha ra k+ki ta'i zhal ldanas pa/ nga bya la ba than dge slong nam mo thos kyis 
271a4(rgyud 'grel): bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o// // mang+ga laM//
